Example keywords you can enter include \"Italy\", \"movies\", \"news\", \"sports\" or any keword that represents the type of television channels you want the app to create for you.\r\n\r\nShortly after, a message will pop up to let you know how many live TV streaming URLs it counted in the free M3U playlists it collected and give you an estimate of the processing time. Each live TV streaming URL is tested for validity.\r\n\r\nThe search can be configured by Country, Language and Depth. Depth represents the extent of the search. If a Depth 1 search does not generate enough channels, try a higher number. Be aware that even a Depth 1 search can take a long time but the estimate will be given in the pop-up message mentioned earlier.\r\n\r\n2) Do your own search\r\n\r\nUse Google from inside the app to target specific web pages with live TV streaming links.
